   168→async function loadSample(type: 'resume' | 'letter') {

   177→async function formatDocument() {
   178→  validationMessage.value = ''
   179→
   180→  if (!textContent.value.trim()) return
   181→

   184→    return
   185→  }

   203→  }

   211→  }
   212→  finally {
   213→    isFormatting.value = false
   214→  }
   215→}

    31→<script setup lang="ts">
    32→import { ref, computed, watch } from 'vue'
    33→import './resume-styles.css'
    34→
    35→defineOptions({ name: 'PreviewPanel' })
    36→
    37→interface Props {
    38→  xmlContent: string
    39→  zoom?: number
    40→}
    41→
    42→const props = withDefaults(defineProps<Props>(), { zoom: 1 })
    43→
    44→const sanitizedHtml = ref<string>('')
    45→const error = ref<string | undefined>(undefined)
    46→
    47→const containerStyle = computed(() => ({
    48→  transform: `scale(${props.zoom})`,
    49→  transformOrigin: 'top left',
    50→}))
    51→
    52→const ALLOWED_TAGS = [
    53→  // Resume elements
    54→  'document', 'header', 'name', 'contact', 'email', 'phone', 'location',
    55→  'linkedin', 'website', 'summary', 'experience', 'role', 'title', 'company',
    56→  'period', 'bullets', 'bullet', 'education', 'degree', 'school', 'year',

    60→  // Standard HTML tags DOMPurify allows anyway — kept for section labels
    61→  'section', 'h2', 'p', 'ul', 'li', 'a', 'br', 'strong', 'em',
    62→]
    63→
    64→const ALLOWED_ATTR = ['type', 'href']
    65→
    66→async function updatePreview() {
    67→  error.value = undefined
    68→  sanitizedHtml.value = ''
    69→
    70→  if (!props.xmlContent) return
    71→
    72→  try {
    73→    // DOMPurify is browser-only — import lazily to avoid SSR issues
    74→    const DOMPurify = (await import('dompurify')).default
    75→    const clean = DOMPurify.sanitize(props.xmlContent, {
    76→      ADD_TAGS: ALLOWED_TAGS,
    77→      ADD_ATTR: ALLOWED_ATTR,
    78→      FORCE_BODY: false,
    79→    })
    80→    sanitizedHtml.value = clean
    81→  }
    82→  catch (err) {
    83→    error.value = err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Could not render document'
    84→  }
    85→}
    86→
    87→watch(() => props.xmlContent, updatePreview, { immediate: true })

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #66
Now let me also check if the AppHeader component in index.vue is importing correctly. In index.vue, the AppHeader is used as `<AppHeader class="app-header no-print">`. But now AppHeader.vue's root element doesn't have the `.app-header` class anymore. The classes from the `class` attribute on `<AppHeader ...>` in the parent will be merged with the root element of AppHeader. Let me also check - in index.vue, the CSS has: ```css .app-container { display: flex; flex-direction: column; height: 100vh; width: 100vw; overflow: hidden; background: #f1f5f9; } ``` This sets the app container to flex column. The AppHeader should take up its natural height, and the dual-panel-layout should flex: 1 to fill the rest. Looking at the structure, the `.dual-panel-layout` needs `flex: 1` and `min-height: 0` to properly fill the remaining space and allow its children to scroll independently. Now I'm checking how the AppHeader component receives classes from the parent. When AppHeader is used with `class="app-header no-print"`, those classes merge onto the root element, which already has `class="app-header"` defined in the template. The duplication is harmless, though the class applied from the parent doesn't actually affect styling since there's no corresponding CSS rule in index.vue for it. The key issue is ensuring the header doesn't shrink when the panels flex. I've added `flex-shrink: 0` to AppHeader's root element, and the dual-panel-layout has `flex: 1` which should work correctly since the app-container is a flex column. Now I'm checking whether the scoped CSS from AppHeader.vue will properly apply the `flex-shrink: 0` style to the root element when it's rendered in the parent component. Vue 3 falls through class inheritance to the root element. When you add a `class` attribute to a component in the template, those classes merge onto the component's root element, which then has both its own scoped styles and the inherited classes from the parent. The root element gets the component's `data-v-XXXX` attribute for its own scoped CSS matching, while inherited classes carry the parent's `data-v-YYYY` attribute. So in this case, even though the parent component passes `.app-header no-print` classes, the parent's scoped styles don't have rules for `.app-header`, so those don't apply. But the child component (AppHeader.vue) has `.app-header` styles in its scoped CSS that target `[data-v-child-hash]`, and since the root element has that attribute, the styles match correctly. Now I need to verify the export-hint text color works properly with the dark header. Still writing styles... Adjusting the text colors for the dark header background — the export hint needs to be lighter so it's readable against the dark background, and I should update the divergence warning text color as well. Adjusting the text color for the export hint to ensure it's readable on the dark background — `#64748b` might work but I should probably go with something slightly lighter like `#94a3b8` to be safe. The divergence info badge should be fine since it has its own background styling that will stand out as a floating element.

The page looks unfinished — plain white, no visual hierarchy, no branding beyond the title. The yellow warning banner (Some content may have been changed) shows every time and feels alarming.

1. Professional page layout — proper spacing, typography, color scheme

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #117
## Status DONE ## What Changed - `components/AppHeader.vue` — Replaced minimal gray header with a dark slate (#0f172a) header featuring bold OhMyDoc branding and a descriptive tagline - `pages/index.vue` — Updated app background to off-white (#f1f5f9), white editor panel, blue-gray canvas (#e2e8f0) for preview, replaced amber warning with blue info badge and softer copy, polished typography and spacing throughout - `components/PreviewPanel.vue` — Made background transparent so the parent canvas color shows through; updated placeholder text color - `components/resume-styles.css` — Added subtle `box-shadow` and `border-radius` to the `<document>` element so the formatted page visually "floats" on the canvas ## Key Decisions - Chose a **dark slate header** over white — creates authority and makes the app instantly feel like a professional tool rather than a prototype - **Warning banner → info badge**: kept the same `divergence > 0.05` threshold (changing it would require understanding the divergence metric better) but changed tone entirely — blue/calm instead of amber/alarming - Font changed from `ui-monospace` to `ui-sans-serif` in the textarea — monospace was appropriate for XML editors (the old approach) but feels clinical for plain-text input ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feature/frg-251-visual-polish` - PR: https://github.com/kimwwk/ohmydoc-using-claude-code-agent/pull/39
